Flickinger University of Iowa</page><page sequence="3">PREFACE At the Nashville meeting in 1928 the Executive Committee on the suggestion of Dr. Roy C. Flickinger took the necessary steps to have an Index of the first twenty-five volumes of the Classicai, Journal published as soon as possible after the completion of the twenty-fifth volume. The editors-in-chief were charged with the management of the enterprise and asked the undersigned to un dertake the preparation of the Index. In order to adopt an approved policy to determine the scope and character of an acceptable and useful index a questionnaire was submitted to the members of the Executive Committee and to others who were by experience competent to give advice in such matters. Guided by the answers returned the indexer adopted a policy leaning toward profuseness, but with an eye to strict economy by omitting details which, desirable in themselves, would add to the cost of production in a degree disproportionate to the value which they might add to the usefulness of the Index. As it is, we believe that nothing important has been omitted and that the Index makes readily available the great wealth of scholarly output and pedagogical discussion which has appeared in the Journal during the past quarter of a century. The only abbreviation which requires explanation is Rev. = "Reviewed." The roster of officers of the Association and of the editors of the Classical Journal, to be found on the last pages of the book, will constitute a monument to those men and women who have unselfishly given their services to the work of the Association and to the making of the Journal. University of Iowa December 1, 1930 Franklin H.
